US Neutrality Act Amendment Introduced to Senate Foreign Relations Committee

Washington: Biderman, chairman of the Senate Foreign Relations Committee, yesterday afternoon invited Democratic members who favored repealing the arms embargo clause to discuss the Neutrality Act amendment drafted by him. Afterwards, it was submitted to the secretariat of the committee today as a basis for discussion. It is heard that there are four main points: (1) Repeal the arms embargo clause; (2) Apply the "cash-and-carry" clause uniformly to the transportation of various goods to belligerent countries; (3) Severely punish those who violate the Neutrality Act; (4) Restrictions must be placed on the granting of commercial credit to belligerent countries. Regarding this point, the current Neutrality Act stipulates that US citizens can still grant "normal short-term commercial credit" to belligerent countries. There are many congressmen who advocate maintaining this provision. Biderman's proposal is likely to arouse strong opposition. (Havas telegram of the 25th)

British Intelligence Agency Refutes German Claims

London: According to the intelligence agency, although the German Foreign Ministry's recently published documents on the final stage of the German-Polish dispute have been disguised in many ways, it is difficult to erase the truth or blame others for the war. The German government did not mention a word about the illegal appointment of Forster, the leader of the Nazi Party in Danzig, as the head of the Free City of Danzig, or the fact that the British government had opposed Germany from the beginning using an ultimatum to demand that Polish representatives must arrive in Berlin by midnight on August 30 to receive the proposal. Germany then said that it had delivered its proposals to the British Ambassador Henderson and explained it in detail to him, but did not specify the date. Germany criticized Britain for rejecting Italy's mediation, but also explained that Britain had stated that it would refuse negotiations unless Germany stopped attacking Poland and agreed to withdraw German troops from Polish territory. In this German document, the meetings between the British Ambassador and Hitler on August 23, 25, 28, and 29, and the meetings between the British Ambassador and German Foreign Minister Ribbentrop on the evenings of August 30 and 31 are not mentioned. Therefore, the content does not seem very accurate. The reason why Hitler and Ribbentrop did not show the people the situation in the country during these two days is very obvious. They have various motivations and do not want to show the German people and the world the truth, that is, that the crisis was caused by Germany's actions. (Reuters telegram of the 25th)

Swedish and Finnish Cargo Ships Sunk by German Submarines En Route; British Cargo Ship Halsall Also Suffers Disaster

Oslo: The Swedish merchant ship Ballater, weighing 1,500 tons, was sunk by a German submarine with torpedoes 15 miles off Langsund on the southern coast of Norway. A Norwegian torpedo boat saw it and often sent 18 to 20 Swedish sailors ashore. The ship was carrying paper pulp to England. This is the fourth ship sunk by German submarines off the coast of the Scandinavian Peninsula in three days. At the same time, according to Berlin news, German officials agreed with the sinking of two Finnish ships carrying celluloid to the UK at the end of the week, saying that if German submarine captains allowed ships carrying military supplies to sail to the UK, they would be committing treason. (Reuters telegram of the 25th)

Berlin: The British cargo ship "Halsall" was sunk by a German submarine near Cork yesterday. Among the 34 crew members, two women escaped in a lifeboat and 12 were missing. It is said that the ship was attacked without any warning. Three people were shot. (Associated Press telegram of the 25th)

The newspaper stated that the British ships sunk totaled 140,445 tons, accounting for 0.75% of the total tonnage of merchant ships, and the lost fishing boats are not included. The German merchant ships lost accounted for only 0.33% of the total tonnage. (Haitong telegram of the 24th)

The Finnish newspaper "Uusi Suomi" stated that celluloid and wood pulp are not contraband, and it is not appropriate to allow submarine captains to decide what goods are contraband. The Finnish newspaper "Hufvudstadsbladet" stated that it is undoubtedly clear that Finnish ships did not carry contraband. Sweden, as a celluloid exporting country, naturally feels anxious. The "Svenska Dagbladet" stated that the celluloid carried by the ships is not contraband for either Britain or Germany. The "Dagens Nyheter" stated that Germany claimed that it would not interfere with neutral countries' trade, but now it has gone back on its word. The "Aftonbladet" stated that the Swedish authorities intend to request an explanation from the German government regarding this matter. (Havas telegram of the 24th)

Capital of Sweden: The Swedish cargo ship "Gertrud Bratt", carrying a batch of celluloid for papermaking to the UK, was sunk by a German submarine with torpedoes en route. The Swedish newspapers were already very anxious about the sinking of two Finnish ships by German submarines yesterday. Upon hearing this news, they became even more uneasy and indignant, as can be seen in today's newspaper comments. The newspapers all said that celluloid should not be considered contraband, and this item is not included in the German list of contraband. Sweden's interests, which are closely related to foreign trade and survival, will be greatly threatened by German submarine warfare. The "Svenska Dagbladet" stated, "German Navy Commander-in-Chief Raeder recently issued a statement that he would not interfere with the trade of neutral countries. This matter is contrary to the above statement. It seems that most of Sweden's export goods have been included in the German contraband list. Our country's import and export trade will be impossible to maintain in the future." The "Dagens Nyheter" stated, "Celluloid is an important export product of our country, and we should continue to find ways to export it and resolutely resist Germany's claims." (Havas telegram of the 25th)

A Comparative View of the Two European Wars (Continued)

— Chen Chuxiang

For years, Britain's policy of tolerating Hitler was not without reason. She feared France's dominance and took precautions to prevent it. Therefore, she pulled up Germany to restrain France. After Germany and the Soviet Union signed the non-aggression pact, they both indicated that Britain desperately wanted them to be enemies, which was also based on the recognition of Britain's role. In general, if we acknowledge that the Sarajevo incident was the fuse of the previous Great War, and that Germany fought to fulfill its alliance with Austria, and Britain fought to maintain Belgium's neutrality, etc., were all excuses, then we must also acknowledge that the Danzig and Corridor issues were the fuse of this Great War, and that Britain and France fought to fulfill their promise to Poland, and Germany fought to lift the restrictions of the Treaty of Versailles and Poland's mistreatment of Germans, etc., were all excuses. Regardless of their proclaimed war aims, if we consider them comprehensively, it is more appropriate to say that Germany was pursuing a policy of dominance in Europe, which Britain could not tolerate, and France was even more unwilling to sit idly by, leading to the war. This argument seems to imply that Germany is the instigator, but my response is that whether the policy of dominance in Europe should be pursued, and whether Britain should prevent it, are not for me to defend, let alone to take sides.

Before the previous Great War, there had been four crises. This time, it seems that there have not been so many crises. It is also interesting to compare the locations where the crises of the two European wars occurred. The crises of the previous European War, except for the third Balkan crisis that occurred in Europe, the other three did not occur in Europe. The points of contention were all on the opposite side of the Mediterranean Sea, in Africa in the colonies. This time, only Italy's annexation of Abyssinia was outside Europe. If we include it as a crisis, the crises before the previous European War were all clearly caused by the direct conflict of interests between the two main parties, such as the Franco-Italian dispute over Tunisia, the Franco-German dispute over Morocco, and the Austro-Serbian dispute over Bosnia-Herzegovina. The conflicting parties in the various crises that have occurred this time are not so simple. In the Abyssinian incident, Britain stirred up all the members of the League of Nations to oppose Italy. The Spanish Civil War, if it is also called a crisis, is even a recognized small-scale world war. Only the Sudetenland crisis last autumn was relatively similar, but the strength of Germany and Czechoslovakia differed greatly, which was still not as "evenly matched" as the two sides in the previous four crises. However, the Sudetenland dispute is still the best comparison with the Austro-Serbian dispute in the previous war. Serbia was weaker than Austria, and Russia, although it wanted to help it, feared Germany. As a result, it persuaded Serbia to compromise, and Austria, because Serbia had Russia behind it, temporarily satisfied with obtaining Bosnia-Herzegovina. Otherwise, given Austria's usual ambitions, it might not have had to wait until its crown prince was assassinated to take action against Serbia (of course, Germany's permission and assistance were even more important). What is different is that during the Sudetenland crisis, Britain and France sacrificed Czechoslovakia to buy temporary peace in Europe, and later lacked the determination to guarantee it, so Czechoslovakia eventually fell. In this Polish question, if Poland had yielded or Germany had retreated, it would have been very possible to temporarily turn it into a crisis without becoming the fuse of a great war. However, the so-called meaning of Poland's yielding is that Poland would have to sacrifice its exports and access to foreign trade. If it did not have Britain and France behind it, it might have been able to consider it. With Britain and France behind it, and Britain and France believing that they had reached the highest limit of tolerance and had to insist, then Hitler would naturally say that this war was caused by Britain giving Poland a blank check, encouraging it to be tough on Germany. If Germany did not have the stimulant of the German-Soviet Non-Aggression Pact, it might have been able to temporarily retreat a little, but that assumption still has many questions. If what Germany and the Soviet Union concluded was truly a military alliance as rumored outside, Germany could rely on it to offset the mutual assistance between Britain and France to Poland, and even fundamentally eliminate the courage of Britain and France to help Poland. What Germany has obtained now is only to use the Soviet Union's power to jointly destroy Poland so that it can fully deal with Britain and France. Since the Soviet Union has stated that it is still willing to maintain neutrality with Britain and France, whether friction will occur after direct contact between Germany and the Soviet Union is highly questionable. No wonder some people say that Hitler is "working for others," while Stalin is reaping the benefits.

However, Britain and France repeatedly stated that they would abide by their promise to aid Poland, and Hitler himself also assumed that Poland's toughness was caused by Britain's promise to provide assistance in various circumstances. If what he said was really what he thought in his mind, then he would not necessarily be completely mistaken in judging that Britain and France would not intervene in the war. Perhaps he was confident that he would win this war, but we cannot but understand the weaknesses and pains that a dictator cannot express himself. Although he can erase the observance and guarantee of international treaties at any time, a word to the domestic audience is always a word, not to mention that Germany has been sailing smoothly for several years, and the current setbacks would greatly violate its honor and shake the public's faith in the government. From this point of view, we can conclude that the outbreak of this war has its inevitability. Germany wanted to dominate Europe and pursued it, but Britain and France could not tolerate it and aided Poland to resist Germany. Within the first two or three days of the war, the general view was that after Germany achieved its goals in Poland, it would present a fait accompli to Britain and France and request peace talks. Now Britain, France, and Poland have mutually agreed not to make a separate peace, and the Soviet Union, although it has sent troops to divide Poland, Britain and France still claim that they will help Poland until its sovereign rights are fully restored. It can be seen that the possibility of a quick end to this war seems very small. Looking back to the beginning of this century, Austria followed Germany's lead in everything, so its development can be compared to Germany's own development. In addition to Germany's own ambitions, it ultimately could not be compatible with Britain's traditional policy, which led to the war. The events before and after are remotely opposite. Although the saying that history repeats itself is still debatable, it is not too much to say that the evolution of history has a fairly fixed law. In 1914, Germany, Britain, and France were the main actors, and they are still the main actors now, and they are still standing on the opposite sides as before. The direction of the two confrontations is also the same. Poland has replaced the position of Russia in the previous war. The previous war was launched by Austria and Germany, but now it is Germany. However, the direction of actual action is different. The attitude of Russia (Soviet Union) is the most important influence. In the previous war, the German General Staff initially adopted a western offensive policy, wanting to use lightning tactics to first subdue France, and then turn its troops to the east. Therefore, it violated Belgium's permanent neutrality and first launched an offensive on the western front. On the eastern front, it was because the internal affairs of Tsarist Russia were corrupt, and secret mobilization had exceeded two weeks, and it had already announced formal mobilization, but the troops had not yet been concentrated. Because it had nothing to fear from Russia, it only adopted a defensive posture, waiting for work at leisure. This time, Germany's goal was originally Poland, so it adopted the fierce offensive on the eastern border that was the western front in the previous war, while the western border relied on the Siegfried Line as the Great Wall, focusing on defense. In the previous war, Russia attacked East Prussia, but this time its replacement, Poland, was attacked by Germany and the Soviet Union. France was originally beaten, but this time it adopted a posture of hitting people (to be continued).

National Compulsory Education Averages

(Chongqing Special Dispatch) According to statistics from the Ministry of Education on various provinces and cities across the country, there are currently 320,080 elementary schools, 559,534 classes, 702,831 faculty and staff, annual expenditures of 111,915,7569 yuan, and 18,285,129 children receiving compulsory education. According to the national school-age children of 53,091,848, the percentage of school-age children receiving compulsory education and the average number of various items are as follows: (1) The percentage of school-age children who have received compulsory education is 35.09%. (2) The average number of schools per 1,000 square li is 6.92. (3) The average number of children enrolled per 1,000 people is 38.33. (4) The average number of classes per school is 1.75. (5) The average number of children per school is 57.38. (6) The average number of children per class is 32.82. (7) The average number of children taught per teacher is 26.13. (8) The average annual expenditure per child is 6.52.

Tzu Lien Hui Disposes of Children from Disaster-Stricken Educational Institutions

The Joint Disaster Relief Association of Philanthropic Organizations has been handling the work of sheltering refugees and providing relief since the war. People from all walks of life in the city have highly praised it. Because of the difficulty in raising relief funds and the fact that the number of refugees has indeed decreased significantly compared to before, it has been decided to end the operation, giving those refugees who can support themselves funds to dismiss them. However, they are quite troubled by the educational affairs of the adults and refugee children that have been handled. After several consultations, it is reported that a decision has been made. Those who are truly unable to do so but have excellent academic performance will be recommended to transfer to various schools in the city. As for the No. 1 Middle School of the Tzu Yuan Shelter and the Refugee Children's Middle School, preparations are being made to hand them over to the Shanghai Refugee Relief Association.

Hong Kong-Shanghai Inter-Port Competition

The Hong Kong-Shanghai Inter-Port Competition was originally scheduled to be held in Shanghai in November this year, and Hong Kong had already agreed to the request. Recently, the outbreak of the European war has raised this issue for discussion. According to Mr. Huang, "In view of the current situation, it is difficult to decide whether to go or not, because many members of the volunteer army of various associations cannot get away to Shanghai, and military personnel also feel the same difficulty. It is best to wait for a few weeks and listen to Shanghai's opinions before making a decision." Everyone agreed and passed. Regarding the issue of how much time should be added after the Hong Kong-Shanghai Inter-Port Competition ends in a draw, both sides held their own opinions. Hong Kong insisted that 20 minutes be added after the draw (10 minutes for changing fields), while Shanghai insisted that 30 minutes be added (15 minutes for changing fields). Recently, the General Assembly received a letter from Shanghai stating that the Shanghai General Assembly Committee members still insisted on the 15-minute proposal. If Hong Kong's final decision still maintains the original opinion, Shanghai can also accept it. As a result, the Hong Kong committee members passed the proposal to add 20 minutes after the game ended in a draw because the Shanghai side had made concessions.

Harboring Selling Pressure, Foreign Exchange Reverses and Loosens, Sassoon Sells British Gold, Buys American Currency

Yesterday, in the foreign exchange market, HSBC's listed prices showed a half-yuan increase for the Japanese yen, reaching 26.5 yuan, and a 0.25 increase for the Dutch guilder, totaling 11.25 yuan. Other currencies, such as British and American, remained stable. The grey market for British and American currencies had dissipated due to the disappearance of various rumors, which gradually stabilized market sentiment and led to a slight easing of market conditions. However, the morning's opening was slightly soft due to weak sales from non-professional traders. British gold was quoted at 4 shillings 1.5625 pence, and the US dollar at 6.875 yuan. But soon, Shanghai Chinese yarn and cotton merchants, along with Hong Kong Electric, suddenly exerted selling pressure, and the buying interest of a certain bank also improved. As a result, the situation immediately reversed and eased. In the afternoon, further selling pressure came from Hong Kong via telegrams. Although Western merchant Sassoon absorbed some US dollars, the position still felt ample. British gold once traded above 4 shillings 2.8125 pence, and the US dollar also eased to 7.09375 yuan. Chinese merchants suddenly seized the opportunity to switch from selling to buying at low prices, and Sassoon also absorbed US dollars. Therefore, the closing price for British gold was 4 shillings 2.5 pence, and the US dollar at 7.0625 yuan. Compared to last weekend, British gold eased by 0.078125 and the US dollar strengthened by 0.15625. The trend for September and October futures was similar to the spot market. Midway, Western merchant Sassoon suddenly sold British currency and bought US currency at an exchange rate of 3.9761 yuan. Furthermore, American bank Chase Manhattan entered with larger sell orders and exited with smaller buy orders, conducting US dollar swaps with Chinese merchants, with a discount of 0.09375 US dollars, resulting in a monthly interest rate of about 1.35%.

Dutch and Japanese Exchange Rates Lengthen

At the beginning of the morning, there were no telegrams from London with the prices from major firms or Bank of America. London's raw gold remained fixed. Exchange rates for British vs. American and British vs. French remained stable, while British vs. Shanghai decreased by 0.125. American vs. British fell by 0.25, American vs. Shanghai decreased by 0.05, and American vs. French decreased by a small amount of 0.025. The Central Bank's listed prices for various currencies remained the same. The bank's opening spot selling prices were 4 shillings 1.5625 pence for British gold and 6.875 yuan for the US dollar. Compared to last Saturday, British gold was slightly tighter by 0.015625, and the US dollar was slightly softer by 0.03125. After opening, Western merchant Sassoon sold spot British gold to non-professional traders at 4 shillings 1.875 pence, a stable condition. When HSBC's listed prices were announced, Dutch and Japanese currencies lengthened, while the rest remained stable. When the silver equalization tax was announced, there were no increases or decreases. Afterwards, Sassoon suddenly entered spot US dollars at 6.9375 yuan, with an exchange rate of 3.9761 yuan. Later, Chinese yarn and cotton merchants, along with Hong Kong Electric, successively sold spot British gold to non-professional traders such as Chase Manhattan at 4 shillings 1.875 and 2.1875 pence, and spot US dollars at 6.9375 and 7.0625 yuan. At this time, the hardest British gold was traded at over 4 shillings 2.5 pence, so the underlying trend slightly eased. Approaching noon, there were slight September and October swap transactions. Chase Manhattan discounted US dollars by 0.09375 to Chinese merchants for arbitrage, which was about 1.35% monthly interest. Extending to the afternoon close, the bank's spot selling prices were 4 shillings 2.1875 pence for British gold and 7 yuan for the US dollar, compared to the morning opening, British gold eased by 0.0625 and the US dollar hardened by 0.125.

Spot US Dollar Re-emerges at 7 Yuan

In the afternoon market, Hong Kong Electric resold spot Central gold to non-professional traders at 4 shillings 2.5 pence, and sold spot US dollars to non-professional traders such as Sassoon and Chinese merchants at 7.0625 and 7.09375 yuan. At this time, the hardest British gold traded above 4 shillings 2.8125 pence. Later, a Chinese merchant sold October US dollars to a certain bank at 7 yuan. The process remained slightly firm. Extending to the late close, the bank's spot selling prices were 4 shillings 2.5 pence for British gold and 7.0625 yuan for the US dollar. This month's prices were the same as the above prices. Gold Market Initially Rises Then Slightly Weakens, Revolving Around 4,100 Yuan

Yesterday's spot gold grey market conditions initially rose then weakened, with the trend revolving around 4,100 yuan. The various false rumors from the past week began to subside today. However, the final result was a slight downward trend due to the easing of foreign exchange. The opening was encouraged by the slightly tight foreign exchange, reaching a high of 4,120 yuan. Subsequently, due to selling from silversmiths, the price immediately returned to a low of 4,100 yuan. However, soon a Hong Kong group suddenly created a buying trend, forcefully purchasing over 300 taels, and securities firms also frequently absorbed gold, causing the market outlook to strengthen. The price rose to a high of 4,168 yuan. Subsequently, due to the easing of foreign exchange, silversmiths and gold firms competed to aggressively sell, and the securities firms also reversed their position to sell, leading to an unsustainable situation. The price plummeted to 4,080 yuan. At noon, the condition slightly stabilized, closing at 4,115 yuan. In the afternoon, the initial condition was still stable. Subsequently, due to the continued slight easing of foreign exchange, retail appetite suddenly waned. In addition, a certain gold firm tended to sell on behalf of speculators. Although the Hong Kong group still had some buying appetite, the position still felt oversupplied. The price once fell to a low of 4,064 yuan. Later, retail investors took advantage of the low prices to raise the market, and the price rebounded to close at 4,085 yuan, a decrease of 20 yuan compared to last weekend's noon close. Trading was still active throughout the day, with over 1,500 taels traded. Silversmith jewelry gold also fluctuated, ultimately remaining unchanged. Customs gold remained stable.

Spot Small Silver Yuan

However, soon the Hong Kong group revived the buying trend, and the securities firms also tracked and absorbed purchases, causing the market to trend upwards again, soaring by 53 yuan. Securities firms bought twenty taels from money exchange businesses for 4,168 yuan. Subsequently, the Hong Kong group and others stopped buying to observe, and because foreign exchange continued to harden, the securities firms also reversed their position to sell. Silversmiths and a certain gold firm also sold quite forcefully, and the market outlook became unsustainable, soon plummeting by 88 yuan. Cash firms sold ten taels to money exchange businesses for 4,080 yuan. Later, as foreign exchange stabilized, the selling trend of silversmiths and a certain gold firm slightly subsided, so general retail investors took advantage of the low prices to absorb purchases, recovering 50 yuan. Money exchange businesses bought ten taels from silversmiths, still at 4,115 yuan. Yarn and Cotton

Industry Stockpiling, Cotton Prices Expected to Rise

The trading of native cotton white packages was still fairly weak. Factory Shenxin and other factories had slightly improved appetite, but the amount consumed was not expanded. Japanese merchants were also in a wait-and-see attitude. Industry sentiment was firm. Although the current source of Tongzhou cotton was still actively arriving, difficulties had occurred in the Huangpu River. Generally, people were worried about future risks. Therefore, a certain cotton firm's intention suddenly changed course. For goods with excellent quality, the opening price was 150 yuan, which was 7 yuan higher than the previous day. It exclusively consumed several thousand packages, flocking to the stacks to stockpile and wait for prices to rise. Cotton prices with slightly inferior quality and moist cotton were still stable. Over 3,200 packages of Tong cotton continued to arrive from Subei, 800-900 packages from Changyinsha, and 1,500 packages from Beisha. The current cotton opening price list is on the left.

In other news, the foreign cotton trading in Shanghai yesterday did not have much change. However, the inventory in Shanghai was not high, so the cotton price reversed to be high. The willingness of industry members to sell was very loose, and they were temporarily unwilling to sell. Currently, raw materials above 32 counts were very rare in the market. Industry members had a small amount of spot goods, but they were not planning to sell them. Factories had a very strong need for this type of cotton, and it was very difficult to purchase. Yesterday, the market price for American species new special cotton that could spin 20 counts was over 190 yuan, and the White Rock price was 172 yuan.

Foreign Cotton Market Prices: The New York cotton market was relatively calm yesterday. Because exporters were not active, the market was unusually stagnant. Later, because some bulls settled and industry members slightly sold off, the result was a closing price that fell by 6-7 pounds compared to the previous day. The Indian cotton market fell 6 rupees including forecasts. The Egyptian Liverpool market was closed.

Coarse Yarn Sales Are Active

The yarn market is still firm, but the rising trend feels more gradual. In fact, part of the psychology is that its bottom has already been high, and the amount of funds has been reduced. Therefore, the rising power of upper-body yarn prices is gentle. However, the prices of medium-count yarns are relatively cheap, so they are slowly rising. For the 10-count coarse yarn of the guest group and Hong Kong group, sales are smooth. Because the price distance from 20-count yarn is too far, and it is also the peak season, market transactions have greatly increased. The profits of factories are not as thick as fine yarns, and they are relatively thin.

After the spurious police invaded the roads built beyond the boundary in West Shanghai and ran amok, causing trouble repeatedly, a public bus driver was kidnapped by thugs in Caojiadu the day before. The Shanghai Municipal Council Police Department instructed the local police station to take stricter precautions in the important areas of the roads built beyond the boundary, causing the situation in West Shanghai to become tense again. Detailed reports are as follows:

Minor Incident Leads to Detention

According to the Continental News, an American Marine from the Fourth Regiment was detained by "Avenue" police in West Shanghai at 9:00 PM last night (the 24th) for a few hours, and was not released until 10:55 PM. The incident occurred in front of the Wellcome Café near Zhaofeng. As of late last night, the details were still unknown, but it is known that the American soldier had an argument with someone. The café's hired usher blew a whistle, and twenty "Avenue" police officers went to the scene upon hearing the sound. They then got into a struggle with the American soldier. The American soldier was outnumbered and overpowered, and was put on a truck and driven to the "Avenue" police station on Jessfield Road.

Released After Two Hours

The Public Concession Police Department and the Fourth Regiment of the U.S. Marines were immediately notified and began discussing the release of the soldier. After several hours of discussion, the American soldier was released. The U.S. Navy and Marine Corps authorities feared that such incidents would continue to occur, so they immediately prohibited Marine soldiers and sailors from going to the Yu Garden Road area, and dispatched patrols throughout the area, ordering all sailors and Marine soldiers to leave. As a result, after 1:00 AM, the taverns and bars and apple game stores near Zhaofeng Park on Yu Garden Road had very few customers.

According to the English-language Great American Evening Post, an American Marine was detained by "Avenue" police on Yu Garden Road last night. Unwilling to Conduct Investigation or Negotiation

Starting the day before yesterday, two Japanese soldiers were dispatched by the Japanese side to suppress the crowds. Yesterday, two "Avenue Police" were added. One of the Japanese soldiers also held a rattan whip and waved it at any time to drive away idlers watching nearby.

Defense of North Henan Road Remains Unchanged

The former British military garrison at the intersection of North Jiangxi Road and Bazih Road and the Railway Hospital at the west end of the road have not been occupied by the Japanese army. At the iron gate at the end of North Henan Road, in addition to the British soldiers still guarding the post, British soldiers are also stationed in the bunker on the right side. At the entrance of Qianjiang Hall at the intersection of North Henan Road and Haining Road, there is a barbed wire frame, and a British soldier is stationed there. As for the situation on the roads between North Jiangxi Road and North Henan Road, everything is as usual.

Southern City Refugee Area: Starting to Adjust Refugee Relief, Quota Set at 20,000 People, Registration Begins, Father Jacquin Attends Office Regardless of Weather

Regarding the recent situation of refugees in the Southern City, according to a report yesterday from a certain gentleman at the branch office of the Southern City Refugee Area Supervisory Committee, the details are as follows:

Southern City Refugees: Nearly 20,000 People

When Shanghai first experienced hardship, Father Jacquin, based on his humanitarian standpoint and past experience, organized the accommodation of refugees from the Southern City, with numbers exceeding 100,000. Subsequently, with the westward movement of the National Army, approximately eight-tenths of the refugees have left Shanghai voluntarily or been evacuated over the past two years. Currently, there are 19,209 refugees (including 10,197 men, 5,204 women, and 3,708 child refugees). There are also 19,700 residents of the area who have been affected by the war and are also provided with relief equivalent to that given to the refugees, but they do not reside in the shelters.

88 Shelters Established

A total of 88 refugee shelters have been established in the Southern City, mostly in public places. The hygiene management and various facilities are generally satisfactory. However, due to the special circumstances, the education of child refugees has not been as widespread as the establishment of schools in the concession shelters. Each refugee is provided with six taels of rice per day. To ensure the health of the refugees, the Southern City First Hospital and Cian Hospital provide daily medical care and medicine to the refugees.

Economic Resources are Very Depleted

As for economic resources, these rely solely on donations from charitable organizations and individuals, as well as a portion of the surplus from French merchant charity lottery tickets. Therefore, the economy is severely depleted. Starting from September 13, the relief provided to residents of the Southern City will be reduced by half (three taels per day) since most residents in the area have jobs and a basic livelihood sufficient to sustain them. Starting from October 1, it is planned to set the quota for refugees at 20,000 people, and registration is now underway to adjust the arrangements. If investigations reveal that there are residents who genuinely cannot sustain their lives, they will still be provided with relief, and it is planned to establish another shelter.

Current Relief Cost is 70,000 Yuan

Furthermore, an investigation reveals that the existing number of refugees is in a dire situation and cannot be reduced further. The monthly relief cost cannot be determined precisely due to fluctuating rice prices, but it is currently around 70,000 yuan. Father Jacquin attends the office daily regardless of the weather and frequently inspects the various shelters. His spirit of humanitarian service is deeply commendable.

Page 10

After the Price Stabilization Ends, Rice Prices Rise Again Yesterday, The Prohibition Order on Tribute Rice Has Not Been Lifted, and National Rice Continues to Arrive, There is No Consideration for a Second Round of Price Stabilization

The price stabilization operation has ended. Mr. Yu Qiaqing said that he considers this price stabilization to be very satisfactory. The gentlemen of the Rice Merchants' Guild have sacrificed their time and effort for the public good, which is truly commendable. Regarding the process and accounts of the price stabilization, the guild will publish them to the public soon. However, seeing the crowded situation of civilians rushing to buy rice, he deeply regrets that it was a drop in the bucket and could not benefit everyone universally. Originally, it was intended to discuss and proceed with another round of price stabilization, but since the origin of tribute rice has not lifted the export prohibition order, and national rice will also arrive continuously, the price of rice is bound to fall, and there is no need to consider it for the time being. He has not heard about the previous rumors that various groups will issue medals to the staff of each price stabilization center to commend them.

Transfer Completed, Scheduled Review

The five tribute rice price stabilization centers in the two concessions have all concluded, and all transfer procedures have been completed. All items used in each center, such as measures and containers, have been returned to the Shanghai Rice Merchants' Guild. In addition to the rice sold and the funds received, which were reported yesterday, the reporter of the New Voice News has further investigated and recorded the following: the five tribute rice price stabilization centers experienced a total loss of 197 piculs of tribute rice and residual rice. The first center had a loss of 100 catties of leftover rice, the second center 293 catties, the third center 354 catties, the fourth center 147 catties, and the fifth center 157 catties. In addition, the first center had 31 catties of other leftover rice, and the fifth center had 100 catties of rotten rice. Together with the cost of the hemp bags, they were all taken back by the association's supervisors. According to the fourth center, 12,000 one-dou tickets and 10,990 five-sheng tickets were sold, but there was one one-dou ticket and two five-sheng tickets, totaling six yuan, for which rice had not been collected. Because the rice has been completely measured, the six yuan has been left for the rice seller to collect upon verification with the original rice tickets. To be accurate, the one-dou tickets should be changed to 11,998 tickets, and the five-sheng tickets should be changed to 10,988 tickets. Now that the Shanghai Rice Merchants' Guild has completely concluded the five tribute rice price stabilization centers, it is scheduled to convene a meeting of the directors of the five centers after the Mid-Autumn Festival to review the conclusion matters.

Announcement of the Conclusion of Broken Rice Price Stabilization

Regarding the price stabilization of 1,000 bags of broken rice in the four price stabilization centers, all were sold out on the 24th. The total amount of rice sold by each center was 1184 piculs and 2 dou, with a loss of 43 piculs, 2 dou, 8 sheng, and 5 shao, 6 catties of extra broken rice, and 10 catties of leftover rice. The association's supervisors have taken back all of them. The total revenue from the sales was 16,578.8 yuan in national currency. The second center has sold broken rice tickets that have not been collected, and the rice has been left in the guild for purchasers to collect with their tickets. Furthermore, there was a discrepancy in the figures reported yesterday by the fifth center, with 800 one-dou tickets and 4,356 five-sheng tickets sold. This morning, the reporter of the New Voice News visited Qu Zhenhua, the executive committee member of the Rice Merchants' Guild, at the bean and rice market. According to Mr. Qu, the decision to carry out the tribute rice price stabilization was due to the scarcity of rice (8,000 bags), which was not enough to solve the problem. However, the fluctuating price of rice recently has had a significant impact on people's food. To stabilize the rice market, it is essential to facilitate the source of national rice, increase reserves, eliminate hoarding, and encourage price reductions. In the rice-producing areas, new crops have already entered the market. He is actively engaging in negotiations to facilitate the flow of national rice, and it is expected that a large amount of national rice will be shipped to Shanghai in the short term. It is reported that the price of rice rose again yesterday.

Rice Prices Rose by One Yuan Yesterday

Yesterday, merchants registered a total of 4,287 bags of rice for sale at the Rice Market Management Committee. A total of 200 piculs of river cargo arrived. Due to the impact of the end of the price stabilization, the market outlook was higher, and prices rose again. White japonica rice rose by half a yuan per picul, with the highest price being 37 yuan per picul. Changshu and Wuxi new indica rice also rose again, reaching nearly 26 yuan per picul. The highest price for Jiangbei indica rice was originally only 23 yuan per picul, but it has also risen again.

Busy Settlement Before the Mid-Autumn Festival

The Time for Acceptance and Payment at the Check Clearing House and Reserve Treasury is Extended

Because tomorrow is the Mid-Autumn Festival in the lunar calendar, all factories, businesses, trading firms, companies, and Shanghai-based offices of various places in the city should, following commercial practice, settle the accounts with all parties and the receivables and payables before this Mid-Autumn Festival, adhering to the old practice without change. After the Mid-Autumn Festival, the accounts of business transactions will be renewed. The receipts and payments of commercial transactions are now mainly based on cash (legal tender) and checks (checks, banker's drafts, remittances, etc.). There are unusually high volumes of mutual receipts and payments. The settlement procedures handled by the Central Bank of China, the Agricultural Bank of China, various commercial banks, foreign banks, and major remittance offices have become extremely busy. The volume of receipts and payments has increased several times compared to normal days. The check clearing house for the silver and money industries and the reserve treasury of the money industry association are the central hubs for the settlement of merchants, and the office hours and time for accepting and paying checks have been invisibly extended.

Fierce Battles Continue in the Territory of Chuansha County, Both Chinese and Japanese Troops Have Casualties, Multiple Japanese Planes Flew to Provide Assistance Yesterday

After Xu Zhidao, the Special Commissioner of the Pudong Loyalty and National Salvation Army Free Army, took office, he has now completed the reorganization of various units and actively strengthened his forces. Therefore, the Japanese side pays special attention to him. The Pudong war, which had been dormant, has become fierce again. According to people from Pudong who arrived in Shanghai yesterday, the Japanese side had recently dispatched

a team of about 150 Japanese soldiers with light and heavy weapons, attacking Huangjialu and Datieqiao in two routes. This area is the defense zone of Xu Chengde, under Xu Zhidao. After Xu learned of this, he quickly assigned the first company to the south of Datieqiao, the second company to defend the Niuduzi area, the third company to be responsible for Huangjialu, and the fourth company to the Liuzaogang area. At the same time, they counterattacked the Japanese troops advancing on the highway. For a time, the fighting was fierce, and the sound of small mortars

lasted for eight hours before stopping. Then, because it was inconvenient for Xu's troops to defend Laogang to the death, they retreated to the west of Erzaohong, holding strongholds in the outer river and pond areas. After a short rest, they again divided into teams to counterattack west from Laogang. The battle is still ongoing. It is reported that the Japanese side suffered heavy casualties in this battle. On the National Army side, officer Han Shulin was killed, and soldiers Liang Zhifa, Yang Deming, Li Shoudao, Qiu Mingqing, Xu Dechang, and messenger Yang Jinrong were wounded. Commander Xu

has provided compensation, with a bonus of 10 yuan for each wounded soldier, 20 yuan for each wounded officer, and a burial fee of 20 yuan for each soldier killed, to show his appreciation. Yesterday morning, several Japanese planes, carrying bombs, went to assist in the fighting.

Expansion of the Double Tenth Festival Disaster Relief Campaign

The Public Unanimously Supports the Cause, Donations Continue for Another Year

October 10th is the 28th anniversary of the founding of the Republic of China. Xu Shiying, Chairman of the Central Relief Committee, will launch a disaster relief campaign throughout the country on that day to raise funds to provide relief to compatriots in distress. According to reporters from the Daguang News Agency, the various groups in Shanghai greatly agree with Mr. Xu's proposal. As the Double Tenth Festival is approaching, they are currently exchanging ideas and preparing to expand the campaign. They also plan to send personnel to visit refugees in various shelters. The public in all sectors believes that in this extraordinary period, when the country is in great difficulty, and considering Shanghai's unique environment, they do not plan to splurge on the Double Tenth Festival or hold celebratory ceremonies. Their belief in the War of Resistance and National Construction is even more steadfast. In addition to the city uniformly raising flags and taking a day off, they are determined to enthusiastically support the disaster relief campaign. Businesses and other sectors that originally pledged to support refugees and donate to disaster relief, although the one-year period has expired, are mostly voluntarily continuing for another year to maintain the relief provided to refugees and stabilize the order of the isolated island.

British Public Bus Company Issues New Tokens

Two Types Available: Nickel Five-Cent and Three-Cent Tokens

According to Datong News Agency, the British China Public Bus Company, in view of the shortage of copper coins and the difficulty in making change in the city, which has caused many obstacles for ticket vendors, has specially manufactured two types of nickel tokens. Their size and shape are different from those previously issued by the company. The five-cent tokens have the Arabic numeral "5" on the front, surrounded by several circles. On the back, there is an engraving of a bus and the company's name in English. The other type, the three-cent token, is also made of nickel but is smaller. Otherwise, it is the same as the five-cent token.

Japan's Import and Export Trade Fails to Recover, Imports and Exports of Yen Bloc Countries Show No Progress in Eight Months

According to the English-language "Great American Evening Post," Japan has tried to increase imports and reduce exports to other countries in the Yen Bloc this year, but has not achieved any results. In the first eight months of this year, Japan's exports to Yen Bloc countries increased by 35.2 million yen, while imports from Yen Bloc countries increased by only 7.16 million yen. From January to August this year, Japan's exports to Manchuria, the Kwantung Leased Territory, China, and Hong Kong totaled 108 million yen, but imports from these four places totaled only 46.5 million yen.

Appeal Debate in the Case of Notorious Bandit Ta Yongkuan and His Son, Verdict Scheduled for the 30th of this Month

Li Yongkuan, Li Jia Zhou, Li Bihua (erroneously reported as Hua), three bandits from Anhui Province, notorious salt smugglers, taking advantage of the westward retreat of the National Army in the winter of the year before last, gathered bandits in the Ruanxiang area of Songjiang, claiming to be guerrillas, and set fire, killed, looted property, and raped women everywhere. They also forcibly robbed two women, Lin Xiuhua and She Yuexian, from Xihutang, and forced them to marry Jia Zhou and Bihua as wives. Li Jia Zhou then shot and killed Lin's mother and buried her. Li Yongkuan, claiming that the Lin family had no descendants, sold Lin's house to a local bully, Lu Baoren. At the end of last spring, they were disarmed by the regular army. Unable to gain a foothold, Li and his family, along with the two women,

fled to Shanghai and hid in Xujiahui in western Shanghai, confining Lin and She and prohibiting them from moving freely. Until last December, the two women escaped and reported to the French police, who arrested Li and the other three people one after another. Stolen goods, such as leather clothing, gold bracelets, and gold rings from the Lin and She families, were found in their home and sent to the Second Special Court. After investigation, the French Concession authorities filed a public prosecution against them for robbery, murder, rape, and illegal detention. Lin and She also filed an incidental civil suit, each requesting 8,000 yuan in consolation money and 500 yuan for Lin's mother's funeral expenses. Because Li and others committed crimes in the interior, regarding the issue of jurisdiction, the Second Special Court submitted a request to the Third Higher Branch Court, which then submitted it to the Supreme Court, designating the Second Special Court

to hear the case. As a result of the trial, on the 16th of last month, Li Yongkuan was sentenced to twelve years of imprisonment for continuous robbery and ten years of deprivation of civil rights. Li Jia Zhou was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for continuous robbery, five years of imprisonment for rape, and fifteen years of imprisonment for murder, to be served concurrently for eighteen years, and fifteen years of deprivation of civil rights. Li Bihua was sentenced to eight years of imprisonment for continuous robbery and five years of imprisonment for rape, to be served concurrently for ten years, and eight years of deprivation of civil rights. The incidental civil suit was transferred to the civil court for trial. Regarding the civil suit portion, it has been concluded by the civil court. On the 23rd of this month, a verdict was issued ordering Li Jia Zhou and Li Bihua to each compensate Lin Xiuhua and She Yuexian 800 yuan in national currency. Li Jia Zhou also had to bear 200 yuan for Lin's mother's funeral expenses. All these details have been recorded in this newspaper. Because Li

and his three sons were dissatisfied with the criminal verdict of the Second Special Court in the first trial, they jointly retained lawyers Fan Gang and Yu Enliang as agents to file an appeal with the Third Higher Branch Court. Yesterday morning, presiding Judge Wu Tingqi, along with Judges Gu Hongbiao and Xiang Zu, and Prosecutor Zhao Changmin, convened a joint trial. According to the reasons for the appeal stated by Li and his sons, they did not believe that the looting and robbery were such. They claim that, with Lu Baoren and Cai Dingyi, the local town leaders, as matchmakers, they married Lin Xiuhua and She Yuexian as daughters-in-law. It was only after arriving in Shanghai that Lin and She were instigated by others to falsely accuse them of robbery and murder, resulting in severe sentences.

They requested a clear investigation, the revocation of the original judgment, and a declaration of innocence. Then, the original plaintiffs, Lin Xiuhua and Yu Yuexian, stated the circumstances of being robbed, forced into marriage, and the three robberies in their home, as well as the process of Li Jia Zhou killing Lin's mother. The court also summoned witness Zhang Hongkui and the investigating detective for questioning. As the details of the case were clear, the court ordered the opening of the debate. First, the prosecutor stated his opinion, saying that it was learned that the appellants had committed such a serious crime during a period of local disorder, and they should be punished severely according to law to deter wrongdoing. The original judgment of imprisonment seemed lenient. He requested the presiding judge to make a judgment according to law. Then, after lawyers Yao Zhaodi of the French Concession authorities and the defense lawyers Fan and Yu debated, the court announced the conclusion of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 30th. The appellants were still returned to the detention center.

Assaulting Mother and Daughter

The Two Convicts Dissatisfied with the Sentence, the Appeal Trial Concluded, Awaiting Judgment

Gu Yang, a woman from Jiangbei living at No. 96, Dakang Lane, Kangdi Road, had a sixteen-year-old daughter, Fendi, who worked in a silk factory. She had to pass in front of the house of her fellow villager, Jiang Xiaosizi (licensed by the Shanghai Municipal Council to operate a cesspit), at No. 152, Xiachengfang, Renshou Lane, Caishi Road, twice a day, morning and evening. Jiang Zimei, the son of Jiang Xiaosizi, was sixteen years old this year. Every time he saw Gu's daughter passing by, he would touch her hands and breasts

and sexually harass her. On the afternoon of July 11th, at 6:00 p.m., when Gu's daughter was returning home from work, passing by Jiang's house, Jiang Zimei again harassed her and hugged her, dragging her into the house. After she struggled and cried out, he released her and she fled home. She cried and told her mother, Gu Yang. That night, the mother and daughter went to Jiang's house to argue, but were beaten and injured by Jiang and his son,

and their clothes were torn. Gu Yang and her daughter then retained lawyers Li Mingzhou and Lian Ze to request an injury examination from the Second Special Court. Afterwards, they filed a private prosecution with the Criminal Court of the Second Special Court against Jiang Xiaosizi and Jiang Zimei for assault and indecent assault, and filed an incidental civil suit, seeking compensation for medical expenses of 60 yuan, 5 jiao, and 4 fen. The defendants retained lawyer Wei Weiqing to defend them and filed a counterclaim

accusing them of defamation. As a result of the initial trial, Jiang Xiaosizi and Jiang Zimei were sentenced to detention for assault, which could be converted to a fine of two yuan per day. Gu Yang's self-accusation against Jiang Zimei and counterclaim were both dismissed. Gu Yang was found not guilty. Because Jiang and his son were dissatisfied with the verdict, they retained lawyer Song Yuntao to file an appeal with the Third Higher Branch Court.

Yesterday afternoon at 3:00 p.m., presiding Judge Wu Tingqi convened a joint trial and summoned both parties and witness No. 332 to the case to question them about the situation at the time. He then announced the conclusion of the trial and scheduled the verdict for the 30th.

New Tricks of the Con Artists, the Spring Lock Scam Fails, Pan Qiliang Arrested While Trying to Escape

Pan Qiliang (24 years old) from Changzhou, and Jiang Shiguang, Zhang the Tea Seller, Qian Boxiang, and others who are at large, usually set up fictitious firms or use a gambling game called "1234" to swindle people out of their property.

There are countless people who have been deceived by them. On the 22nd of this month, Pan and others used the same trick again. They went to Ruicheng Hardware Store in Zunde Lane, Qingmen Road, pretending that they had opened a Dasheng firm in the Jin Yu Inn on Tianzhutang Street in the French Concession. They claimed that they had been entrusted by a merchant to buy twenty dozen new-style spring locks (worth more than 600 yuan), and they would bring the money back as soon as the goods were delivered. Ma Songquan, the manager of the store,

believing them to be true, prepared the goods and ordered his apprentice, Lu Wenqiao, to follow Pan. As soon as they arrived at the inn, two men took the goods, and told Lu to follow Pan to the bank to collect the money. Unexpectedly, Pan seized the opportunity to escape halfway. He was spotted near Maidiyan Road by detectives Ke Enqing and Ke Enhong of the French Concession Police, who, seeing that his

expression was flustered, stepped forward to arrest him. He confessed the truth after being taken to the police station. Therefore, Pan Qiliang was sent to the Criminal Division 8 of the Second Special Court yesterday for investigation. After Judge Zhu examined the case, he ordered a postponement of the hearing for further investigation and arrest of accomplices, as the investigation was still needed. The defendant was returned to custody.

Theft at the Jianye Silk Factory, Suspects Arrested

At around 4:00 a.m. the day before yesterday, more than a dozen armed bandits broke into the back door of the Jianye Silk Factory at No. 551, Tokyo Road, Shanghai West, silenced those who made a sound with guns, and stole six large packages of raw silk (weighing about 130 pounds), worth more than 6,000 yuan, before fleeing with the stolen goods. After reporting the incident to the Gordon Road Police Station, detectives Xu Decheng and Wu Dekui were dispatched to investigate the factory. Chen Aliang, the cook from Shaoxing, Ye Jincai, the cook, and Gao Jinrong, a laborer from Yangzhou, were suspected of colluding with the bandits as insiders. Impersonating the Fire Brigade to Sell Fire Extinguishers: Young Man Guo Yao Arrested

A local young man named Guo Yao (also known as Guo Bianting), impersonated the Shanghai Municipal Council Fire Brigade to print a large number of cards to sell fire extinguishers for the Dahua Fire Prevention Association. He was arrested by Detective Ding Yu and handed over to the Fourth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. He was prosecuted for fraud and other crimes. Judge Fang Qinghuan interrogated him in the courtroom. The defendant, Guo Yao, admitted that he was a salesman for the Dahua Fire Prevention Association, but denied impersonating the Municipal Council Fire Brigade, claiming that the Dahua fire extinguishers were approved for sale by the Fire Brigade and were not illegal. The court then questioned the plaintiff, Ding Yuhua, who testified, "I run a lunch box business. Now, due to rising prices, business is slow, and I cannot afford to install a fire extinguisher. The defendant said he was sent by the Fire Brigade and insisted on installing one for 18 yuan. That's why I called the police. I don't know if he is real or fake." After verifying the statements, the court ordered the defendant to be remanded in custody and adjourned the hearing until next Monday.

Continued Trial of the Moales Case: Testimony of the Autopsy Doctor

According to the English-language "North China Daily News," the case of Moales, an employee of the Municipal Council's Health Department, accused of causing death by negligence, continued its trial this morning (the 25th) at the British Police Court, with Registrar Haines presiding. Dr. Gang Wright testified that on the morning of September 9th, he dissected the body of a Chinese man at the Japanese Marine Corps Hospital. The deceased's face showed evidence of being beaten. An examination of the deceased's heart revealed that it was about twice the normal size due to several diseases. If the deceased had to engage in any strenuous work, these diseases would likely have caused his death within two months. Other witnesses called to court this morning included Mr. Hui of the Public Works Department, who described the terrain of the area, and Mr. Kepenntan of the Health Department, who accompanied the defendant on the night of the incident, also testified about the circumstances of the incident. The defendant's lawyer, Li Kesi, cross-examined the witnesses. The case was adjourned until 10:00 AM on Friday.

Smoking Opium: Sentenced to Six Months Imprisonment, Commutable to a Fine

Ye Meisheng, a Ningbo native residing at the residence of the late Deputy Foreign Minister Tang Youren, is fifty years old. Recently, the Police Department received a tip that his home was an opium trafficking center. Yesterday morning (the 25th), a large number of Chinese and Western detectives were dispatched to surround the entire residence and search it. Ye Meisheng was arrested on the spot, and dozens of taels of opium, dozens of cans of opium paste, two valuable opium pipes, opium lamps, and other items were confiscated and taken to the police station. In the afternoon, he was transferred to the Eighth Criminal Court of the court for prosecution in accordance with the law. Judge Zhu Chuzhe questioned him, and the defendant confessed to smoking opium. The court verified the statements and immediately pronounced the verdict, which stated: "Ye Meisheng is sentenced to six months of imprisonment, deprived of his civil rights for one year, and ordered to quit opium within one month. If he commutes the sentence to a fine, it will be calculated at three yuan per day."

Police Officer Becomes a Bandit: Sentenced to Twelve Years Imprisonment

Li Ziming, a Shandong native who previously served as Chinese Constable No. 774 at the Huishi Police Station, demanded a bribe from Jin Meisheng, the owner of Swallow's Nest at No. 4, Lane 527, Yihua Road, on October 19th of last year. When Jin refused, Li shot and injured him. On the same day, he also shot and injured Yang Ronghua, the doorman of the Shengsheng Trust Company at No. 80 Ningbo Road, and fled his post. On July 8th of this year, Li and his accomplices armed with weapons robbed Yan Yuncheng's home at No. 1297 Yuyuan Road of 20 yuan in legal tender. During their escape, they opened fire on Japanese Constable No. 789 and Chinese Constables No. 2189 and No. 2495 along the way. Li was shot and injured and captured. When he was sent to the First Special Court for trial, Judge Xiao Peishen presided over the Second Criminal Court yesterday morning and sentenced Li Ziming to seven years of imprisonment for conspiring to break into a residence and steal at night with deadly weapons, six years of imprisonment for attempted murder, and seven years of imprisonment for continuous attempted murder, to be served for a total of twelve years. One pistol and four bullets were confiscated and temporarily stored at the police station.

Grand Wedding of Ai Sun

Mr. Ai Weichao, who studied electrical engineering in England and is an outstanding talent in our country's machinery field, currently works as an engineer at the British-owned Wanbao Yangxing in Shanghai. Yesterday, he married Miss Sun Yuanzhen, the eldest daughter of Mr. Sun Liangzheng, at the Moore Memorial Church. Miss Sun graduated from the Department of Sociology at Tsinghua University and has a deep understanding of Chinese and Western cultures. Mr. Ai and Miss Sun were old classmates and are both devout Christians who share the same ideals and are a perfect match. It is said that they will go to Kunming after their marriage to serve the academic community. Yesterday, many prominent figures from the business and academic circles attended, making it a grand occasion.

Letter to the Editor

To the esteemed editor of your newspaper:

Having read the news article "Lawyer Yang Yiming Assaults People, Shops Jointly Provide Proof" in your newspaper on the 21st of this month, it states that Judge Qiu presented the joint public statement signed by more than 30 shop residents of Siyi Village, who witnessed Yang's assault, to Yang for inspection. Yang Yiming then stated in court that since the shop residents had personally witnessed the incident, he requested the court to summon them to appear in court for questioning. Judge Qiu verified the statement and announced that the case would be re-examined at a later date. We are extremely surprised by this. Lawyer Yang Yiming does indeed reside at No. 33 Siyi Village, Huixi Street, Xujiahui, in the same village as the shop residents. However, the shop residents did not actually witness him assaulting Madam Song Wang from Songjiang. How could they have signed a joint public statement? It is clear that unscrupulous individuals are using our names to deceive others. We were about to write a letter requesting a correction when we saw the letter from Lawyer Yang Yiming in your newspaper on the 23rd of this month, which stated that "the truth of the case will be judged fairly, and as for the joint statement from the shops discovered during the trial to be irregular," etc. This confirms that the shop residents have unintentionally offended their neighbor due to the pranks of others, and it is a completely undeserved disaster. This not only fabricates rumors but also concerns personal reputation. Therefore, in addition to waiting to be summoned for questioning, we dare to write this letter for correction and hope that it will be published to clarify the truth for the public. We are deeply grateful for this.

Sincerely,

Representatives of the shops in Siyi Village:

Huang Liansheng, owner of Huixin Shop

Yang Qinshan, owner of Huiji Workshop

Representatives of the residents:

Guo Xihua

Song Yunsheng

The Xujiahui Observatory's weather forecast at 4:30 PM yesterday stated that the weather in Shandong and the East China Sea would change from overcast to cloudy, and rain was likely in some areas. On the same day last year, the highest was 78.4 degrees, and the lowest was 57.0 degrees.

Free Talk

Spark-like Life

— Guo Guo

Sparks - bright, burning. And the life of youth should be like that spark.

The life of youth should be vigorous, full of light and heat; but even so, it is still not enough. We should use the brilliant "light" emitted from our own lives to burn away the dark side of society, so that countless people who have fallen into the black prison can use your "light" to climb out of the black prison; and the huge amount of "heat" emitted in your life should be used to warm those who feel cold, so that they can also generate the same huge amount of heat as a driving force for advancement.

The creation of sparks is due to the collision of two "forces". The idea of living is inherent in human beings, and then, certain improper desires arise. If human beings do not sanction those improper desires and eliminate them, but instead want to satisfy them, then not only will conflicts between people increase as a result, but the justice of the world will also be completely destroyed; the evolution of the world will inevitably stagnate, and may even exceed the barbarity of the primitive era. People have an instinct for doing good: to fully develop what is right, and to sanction and destroy what is wrong. The force that stimulates desire may be unavoidable, but the ability to restrain desire is even more excellent. The encounter and collision of the two "forces" will emit bright, burning sparks in life. This "heat" drives them forward, and this "light" illuminates them to seize great objects. If we give this kind of person a name, then it is "hero". And youth should have a "heroic" life - here, we must recognize that a personal "hero" does not exist, whether for oneself or for the public. We evenly promote these two "forces", make these two "forces" fight fiercely, and make our own lives full of light and heat, like a spark.

The so-called spark-like life is not mysterious, just as the spark itself is not a mysterious thing. Primitive humans saw the fire come and go without fixed time, sometimes seeing it set off a flame that burned the sky, and sometimes seeing the flame disappear without a trace, and felt that this was a mysterious and elusive thing. But thanks to the efforts of scientists, they learned that "fire" is just a phenomenon of combustion, and combustion depends on the support of gases (such as oxygen, etc.). The birth and death of flames are closely related to the amount of oxygen content. In ancient times, humans were "ruled by fire; but in modern times, humans control "fire". Regarding life, we should also take off the mysterious coat. The power of "gods", "ghosts", and "fate" can never shake or control our lives. To fan the flames of our lives, we must first increase the content of "air elements" in our lives. The reason why the flame of a person's life is dim is because the content of "oxygen" in their life is too thin. I dare not say that this is the truth, but the boundary marker between the "bitterness" and "happiness", "fulfillment" and "emptiness" of life is here.

Sparks - bright, burning, and the life of youth should be like that spark.

Love of the River

— Tang Wei

——Records Picked Up From Ashes——

For some reason, I decided to live with Lao Chong.

Our residence is at the end of the street, a board room near the river; this place is very much like the fairy cave in "Liaozhai". Artemisia clings to the three-sided walls, and unknown insects chirp day and night, not allowing you to have a moment of quiet thought; - fortunately, we have escaped the white Russian vagrants and prostitutes. The drunken songs after drinking always make me occasionally hear them, but because they are too far away, I find them vaguely interesting.

The river water by the window is like a mirror lying face up, and the lights render countless mottled golden spots on the water.

I am fascinated by it.

The overlapping ripples, the crane-wing-like shadows of sails, ridiculed me several fire-like rams; I decided to leave it several times, - but soon I appeared again on its floating sand embankment.

Now, the Songhua River also seems to have changed its appearance; its huge figure seems to be a virgin who has just been ravaged, lying tired and in pain.

I can't bear to look at it any longer, and I don't know what force is secretly teasing me! I can't sleep peacefully.

It's late at night.

I walked onto the floating sand embankment again. There was no sound of dust, and I lowered my breath. I gently held up the river water with my hand and kissed it on the mouth - this tender comfort made the river water sob even more deeply.

Across the river, the barking of dogs and the lush villages are beckoning me affectionately in the shadows!

I watched over everything living in this cruel fate until the autumn mist dampened my hair.

It was already dawn when I came back.

Lao Chong told me that this section of the river is often used as a secret execution ground by the port military police at night, and I realized that I had just taken a big risk unknowingly.

Holland Waiting with Spears as Pillows

— Written by Philip Debock, Translated by Wang Baishi

Today's Holland is still as strong as before. Compulsory military service has been further expanded. Every man between the ages of 19 and 55 has the obligation to perform military service. Generally, every 19-year-old youth must undergo eight months of military training. Those with higher education receive even longer training and are commissioned as reserve officers (N.C.Os). From the ages of 19 to 28, they serve in the field army, and after this age, they join the national defense force. Therefore, although Holland has a population of only nine million, it has nearly 800,000 soldiers. These troops are fully trained, well-equipped, and can be mobilized within 24 hours; some (such as those defending the border or coastline) can be concentrated within six hours.

The main component of the Dutch army is the field army - the most elite unit; they are ready to strike at the fierce aggressor at any time.

The Dutch border does not have strong fortifications like the Maginot Line or the Siegfried Line. Furthermore, the border line is too long. To build such fortifications, even for the wealthy Netherlands, would be too expensive. But it cannot be said that Holland has no defenses at all. On the border with Germany and Belgium, many posts and other defensive works are scattered without deviation, surprising neutral observers.

The Dutch army is not used to invade other countries, but to resist aggression. Its defensive line is built according to the natural terrain. Currently, its biggest hypothetical enemy is the German army. The first natural defensive line in the east is the Ysel and Meuse rivers, which flow north and south. West of the Zuider Sea and Maastricht, there are high mountains and steep ridges, forming an exceptionally strong natural defensive line. Even in peacetime, it is firmly guarded. Along the line are many guard posts, dark intercept platforms, and countless solid trenches and other defensive works. The bridge markers on the river are planted with mines in peacetime, so in an emergency, the government in The Hague only needs to give an order, and they can immediately be blown to pieces.

The second defensive line is in the Eem River basin. This is a small river that flows north from Wageningen (on the Rhine River), along Amersfoort, into the Zuider Sea. The entire river passes through a ten-mile-wide plain. This plain is surrounded by large mountains in the east and west. If the Rhine River water or the Zuider Sea water is introduced into this plain, it will immediately become a vast ocean one or two feet deep within one or two hours.

Readers may not be able to imagine how effective this flooding defense line would be. The flooding near Dixmuyde during the last European war can be said to be close to this strategy; however, that was only used as an expedient measure. Holland is now planning it in detail in peacetime, and its effectiveness is of course greater. Holland accurately knows the source of the water, has established many water gates, and people (mostly reserve soldiers) live near the water gates so that they can open the gates at any time. Holland also fully knows the direction of the water flow, the size of the flooded area, and the water depth at each location. In peacetime, they have prepared special maps to mark all of this.

In 1914, the accidental flooding of the Western Front saved the British, French, and Belgian armies from defeat. Therefore, Holland's well-prepared waterlogging strategy can at least strike a blow to the enemy, while greatly helping the country's army defend the motherland, there is no doubt about it. They will then completely flood the ground, with just enough water so that it is too shallow to sail, but deep enough to make it impossible to distinguish between the hundreds of small canals that intersect and cut across the Dutch pastures and the land, greatly hindering the enemy army. The enemy's heavy tanks will be completely ineffective and will have to wade through the mud.

The Dutch military authorities are confident that many flooding defense lines will not be breached by the enemy. However, the people behind the defense line may suffer terrible aerial bombardments, which may lead them to abandon the defense.

Therefore, air defense has become a major issue for Holland. The Dutch Air Force consists of three regiments, and all the aircraft and combatants are very good. Dutch civil aviation has a long-standing reputation in the world.

There is one regiment of anti-aircraft artillery, and the equipment is the latest.

As for maritime defense, Holland relies mainly on submarines, motor torpedo boats, and other small warships. Most of the large warships are used in the Dutch East Indies. These small warships, driven by the famous Dutch sailors, rushing and crashing in the shallow sea, are precisely the vanguards that are difficult for the aggressor to deal with!

Whether Germany dares to break Holland's neutrality and attack it recklessly, who knows?

Heart's Song

— Wen Xi

I wish for a violent storm, a high tide of waves, to drive away the sorrow that lingers in my heart all day long.

I cannot see the smile of youth, nor the enthusiastic surge of young people; everything is followed by shadows.

I feel empty all over, as if I am starving, and I am gradually developing a disgust for this world.

The previous life was in the dark, but sometimes it was also full of happiness. Comparing it with the present, I only get "unbearable memories". Therefore, people build their lives on the "future". This unblown flower bud is placed in a passionate heart and cultivated with all their energy.

The current suffering can only be endured. The dim light is not to be mourned. Even in the darkness, my will cannot be obscured.

I wish for a cup of bitter wine, swallowed into my throat, and the last tear to fall, and then I will say goodbye to pain.

I wish I could sing a few short songs every day, telling my wishes, so that I can have a pure heart and not enter the muddy stream.
